function g__init_form() {
    var $ = jQuery;
    var processed = false;
    tildaForm_send_mock = function(form, btnSubmit, formType, formKey) {
        if (processed) return;
        var form = t_forms__getElement(form)
        var dataForm = t_serializeArray(form);
        var arrFilter = [];
        var dictFilter = {};
        Array.prototype.forEach.call(dataForm, (function(t) {
            -1 === t.name.indexOf("tildadelivery-") && arrFilter.push(t)
            dictFilter[t.name] = t.value
        }
        ))
        dataForm = arrFilter;
        var note = `Partner form: ${window.location.href}`;
        for (i in dataForm) {
            var key = dataForm[i].name
            if (key.startsWith('form') || key.startsWith('tilda') || (key.toLowerCase().indexOf('name') !== -1 && key !== 'Name_3') || (key.toLowerCase().indexOf('phone') !== -1 && key !== 'Phone_2')) {
                continue;
            }
            if (key == 'Name_3') key = 'Имя агента';
            else if (key == 'Phone_2') key = 'Телефон агента'
            note += `\n${key}: ${dataForm[i].value}`;
        }

        var url = new URL(window.location.href);
        data = {
            action: 'partner-custom-form',
            token: 'BnYxulkF_XC5Aq7Re9oO80vbIu-ZblVbALCDNDdAJE0',
            partner_id: 19056,
            name: (dictFilter['Name'] + ' ' + dictFilter['Name_2']).trim(),
            email: dictFilter['Email'] || '',
            phone: dictFilter['Phone'],
            lang: window.location.href.indexOf('/en') === -1 ? 'ua' : 'en',
            note: note,
            utm_source: url.searchParams.get("utm_source") || '',
            utm_medium: url.searchParams.get("utm_medium") || '',
            utm_campaign: url.searchParams.get("utm_campaign") || '',
            utm_term: url.searchParams.get("utm_term") || '',
            utm_content: url.searchParams.get("utm_content") || '',
            utm_referrer: url.searchParams.get("utm_referrer") || '',
            adv_id: 'partners_form'
        }

        if (!data.name) {
            data.name = data.phone;
        }
        if (data.name && data.phone) {
            $.ajax({
                url: 'https://crm.g-plus.app/api/actions',
                method: 'post',
                data: data
            }).done(function() {
                processed = true;
                window.tildaForm.send = tildaForm_send_orig;
                window.tildaForm.send(form, btnSubmit, formType, formKey);
            });
        }
        else {
            tildaForm_send_orig(form, btnSubmit, formType, formKey);
        }
    }
    var replace_interval = setInterval(function() {
        if (window.tildaForm && window.tildaForm.send) {
            tildaForm_send_orig = window.tildaForm.send;
            window.tildaForm.send = tildaForm_send_mock;
            clearInterval(replace_interval);
        }
    }, 200);
}

function g__init_form() {
    var $ = jQuery;
    var processed = false;
    tildaForm_send_mock = function(form, btnSubmit, formType, formKey) {
        if (processed) return;
        var form = t_forms__getElement(form)
        var dataForm = t_serializeArray(form);
        var arrFilter = [];
        var dictFilter = {};
        Array.prototype.forEach.call(dataForm, (function(t) {
            -1 === t.name.indexOf("tildadelivery-") && arrFilter.push(t)
            dictFilter[t.name] = t.value
        }
        ))
        dataForm = arrFilter;
        var note = `Partner form: ${window.location.href}`;
        for (i in dataForm) {
            var key = dataForm[i].name
            if (key.startsWith('form') || key.startsWith('tilda') || (key.toLowerCase().indexOf('name') !== -1 && key !== 'Name_3') || (key.toLowerCase().indexOf('phone') !== -1 && key !== 'Phone_2')) {
                continue;
            }
            if (key == 'Name_3') key = 'Имя агента';
            else if (key == 'Phone_2') key = 'Телефон агента'
            note += `\n${key}: ${dataForm[i].value}`;
        }

        var url = new URL(window.location.href);
        data = {
            action: 'partner-custom-form',
            token: 'BnYxulkF_XC5Aq7Re9oO80vbIu-ZblVbALCDNDdAJE0',
            partner_id: 19056,
            name: (dictFilter['Name'] + ' ' + dictFilter['Name_2']).trim(),
            email: dictFilter['Email'] || '',
            phone: dictFilter['Phone'],
            lang: window.location.href.indexOf('/en') === -1 ? 'ua' : 'en',
            note: note,
            utm_source: url.searchParams.get("utm_source") || '',
            utm_medium: url.searchParams.get("utm_medium") || '',
            utm_campaign: url.searchParams.get("utm_campaign") || '',
            utm_term: url.searchParams.get("utm_term") || '',
            utm_content: url.searchParams.get("utm_content") || '',
            utm_referrer: url.searchParams.get("utm_referrer") || '',
            adv_id: 'partners_form'
        }

        if (!data.name) {
            data.name = data.phone;
        }
        if (data.name && data.phone) {
            $.ajax({
                url: 'https://crm.g-plus.app/api/actions',
                method: 'post',
                data: data
            }).done(function() {
                processed = true;
                window.tildaForm.send = tildaForm_send_orig;
                window.tildaForm.send(form, btnSubmit, formType, formKey);
            });
        }
        else {
            tildaForm_send_orig(form, btnSubmit, formType, formKey);
        }
    }
    var replace_interval = setInterval(function() {
        if (window.tildaForm && window.tildaForm.send) {
            tildaForm_send_orig = window.tildaForm.send;
            window.tildaForm.send = tildaForm_send_mock;
            clearInterval(replace_interval);
        }
    }, 200);
}

function g__init_form() {
    var $ = jQuery;
    var processed = false;
    tildaForm_send_mock = function(form, btnSubmit, formType, formKey) {
        if (processed) return;
        var form = t_forms__getElement(form)
        var dataForm = t_serializeArray(form);
        var arrFilter = [];
        var dictFilter = {};
        Array.prototype.forEach.call(dataForm, (function(t) {
            -1 === t.name.indexOf("tildadelivery-") && arrFilter.push(t)
            dictFilter[t.name] = t.value
        }
        ))
        dataForm = arrFilter;
        var note = `Partner form: ${window.location.href}`;
        for (i in dataForm) {
            var key = dataForm[i].name
            if (key.startsWith('form') || key.startsWith('tilda') || (key.toLowerCase().indexOf('name') !== -1 && key !== 'Name_3') || (key.toLowerCase().indexOf('phone') !== -1 && key !== 'Phone_2')) {
                continue;
            }
            if (key == 'Name_3') key = 'Имя агента';
            else if (key == 'Phone_2') key = 'Телефон агента'
            note += `\n${key}: ${dataForm[i].value}`;
        }

        var url = new URL(window.location.href);
        data = {
            action: 'partner-custom-form',
            token: 'BnYxulkF_XC5Aq7Re9oO80vbIu-ZblVbALCDNDdAJE0',
            partner_id: 19056,
            name: (dictFilter['Name'] + ' ' + dictFilter['Name_2']).trim(),
            email: dictFilter['Email'] || '',
            phone: dictFilter['Phone'],
            lang: window.location.href.indexOf('/en') === -1 ? 'ua' : 'en',
            note: note,
            utm_source: url.searchParams.get("utm_source") || '',
            utm_medium: url.searchParams.get("utm_medium") || '',
            utm_campaign: url.searchParams.get("utm_campaign") || '',
            utm_term: url.searchParams.get("utm_term") || '',
            utm_content: url.searchParams.get("utm_content") || '',
            utm_referrer: url.searchParams.get("utm_referrer") || '',
            adv_id: 'partners_form'
        }

        if (!data.name) {
            data.name = data.phone;
        }
        if (data.name && data.phone) {
            $.ajax({
                url: 'https://crm.g-plus.app/api/actions',
                method: 'post',
                data: data
            }).done(function() {
                processed = true;

            tildaForm_send_orig = window.tildaForm.send;
            window.tildaForm.send = tildaForm_send_mock;

    }, 200);
}
